                                    <!-- SE-TEXT { --><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-38befef4-2cbc-47b0-a070-37f63551ec4e"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-45bd5eea-73ff-4a9a-8860-d57662496ba9">신주쿠에서 하코네까지 가장 빠르고 편안하게 가고 싶다면 단연 </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-d0a53982-e01f-40c2-bfbf-44a020ced028"><b>특급열차 '로망스카'</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-1a18fa94-fd29-440b-b4fd-cd4c2e80f412">입니다. </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-582b96ff-faa8-45c0-bf7f-dafb8417c7db"><b>하코네 프리패스 + 로망스카 특급권 추가구매</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-c4c55b68-0af0-4e3b-9501-2e553ba13c8e"> 하면 전철이 아닌 </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-236eef58-553f-4958-a97e-269719887d67"><b>특급열차</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-d8e71279-f084-4b14-a741-04e80286903b">로 편안하게 이동할 수 있습니다. </span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-a0e4682b-5dc1-4cf6-b18e-cf850ffce027"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-af7dcae5-d2ad-4a0e-8803-abe1486b75b5">특히 로망스카는 오다와라가 아닌</span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-9cbfc1e1-0784-4786-b847-7cbe5cc8b9f1"><b>하코네</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-a859449e-cee8-4c25-af05-0a975e6346fb">할 수 있고 시간도 </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-211368d1-fd14-4432-b0bb-58949c95a8e7"><b>전 좌석 지정제</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-                         <div class="se-section se-section-quotation se-l-quotation_line">
                            <blockquote class="se-quotation-container">
                                <div class="se-module se-module-text se-quote"><!-- SE-TEXT { --><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left " style="" id="SE-edb8a79d-f459-48c1-8ae6-3b5ee6158df6"><span style="" class="se-fs- se-ff-   " id="SE-71251e4b-cba9-416f-b087-688bf8e7bb78"><b>코스 2: 여유로운 1박 2일 료칸 여행 (힐링 끝판왕 코스)</b></span></p><!-- } SE-TEXT --></div>

                <div class="se-component se-text se-l-default" id="SE-407ce71f-200a-4dc8-b5eb-d7837f934c4f">
                    <div class="se-component-content">
                        <div class="se-section se-section-text se-l-default">
                            <div class="se-module se-module-text">
                                    <!-- SE-TEXT { --><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-68d6cc56-180b-47f1-84fc-e2156340a9d4"><span style="color:#000000;" id="SE-b119aa01-9fae-4c31-af1e-14ce8d2c383c"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-53744d36-7eb8-4d1b-a06f-ed2c9260567f">​</span></p><ul class="se-text-list se-text-list-type-bullet-disc"><li class="se-text-list-item"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-5584742c-80be-461f-9786-f4f3e09d179a"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-306c8a50-4a09-484e-b447-d0dd878ae93e"><b>DAY 1:</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-d87a348c-64af-44dd-8758-8652a52f0f1e"> </span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-7b9b7d0f-3aaa-4c64-a869-37a2ab646b70"><b>'당일치기 코스'의 1~7번</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-25864705-7ed3-4c33-86f8-6f9218288458">까지 여유롭게 진행 → 모토하코네항에서 버스로 예약한 료칸 이동 → 체크인 후 뜨끈한 온천과 정갈한</span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-c77807fd-d95c-447b-a1e0-137e07886907"><b> 가이세키 </b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-fe313809-81a7-43e4-b11f-101b2112911d">저녁 식사 즐기기</span></p></li></ul><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-2d7d9a6b-3cf5-4a06-9c3a-aeac0e87ee58"><span class="se-text-list-item"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-f56755a3-b7d0-48c7-9289-2924708faa7a"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-2728da3e-a2f0-4694-bc97-246fe99588f6"><b>DAY 2: </b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-e4f02226-0fb7-4b59-8ecd-3f9a54e63f78">느긋하게 아침 온천 후 조식 → 하코네 조각의 숲 미술관 관람 → 하코네유모토역 근처 맛집에서 점심 → 기념품 쇼핑 후 신주쿠로 복귀</span></p></li></ul><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-e02ef2ab-971c-49ee-85ae-3c159ac67804"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-468106f9-1c4c-4a70-866a-f0f82a83b81e">​</span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-5f0c8617-4ec8-42d6-a6a7-9b872b21688d"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-8d1298f4-2813-4f39-9eb3-49a66a75f45b"><b>하코네 등산 전차 &amp; 조각의 숲 미술관</b></span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-70e3015f-bd43-4b0f-affb-2e221e388298"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-e55f609b-5711-4b5f-9e29-3e159f124329">하코네유모토역에서 빨간색 등산 전차를 타고 여행을 시작합니다. 약 30분 정도 산을 오르다 보면 '조각의 숲' 역에 도착합니다. 역 바로 앞에 위치한 '</span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-dcef0f97-c495-4fd6-99d5-9e99b17b78b7"><b>하코네 조각의 숲 미술관'</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-80678ddb-a865-477e-88be-65dc9d5ae63d">은 하코네의 자연 속에서 거대한 예술 작품들을 감상할 수 있는 곳으로, 하코네 여행의 하이라이트 중 하나입니다.</span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-8f1e5234-dc6a-4cbb-988f-284117bb6bc5"><span style="color:#000000;" id="SE-20070435-1122-4532-9b24-8819226a4e51"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-25638a61-16ca-4f81-b822-2e5e71760280">자세한 입장료 할인 꿀팁과 놓치면 안 될 포토존 정보가 궁금하다면 아래 상세 가이드를 꼭 확인해보세요!</span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-1225bbe4-eb48-4bfb-aac9-dc8fa0283796"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-                                 <div class="se-module se-module-text se-quote"><!-- SE-TEXT { --><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align-left " style="" id="SE-9d4a7ef1-3c2d-4e1d-b7ea-47d76039d83f"><span style="color:#aa1f91;" class="se-fs-fs24 se-ff-   " id="SE-0d33c763-ca8f-49aa-86e3-89bdeb724a5e"><b>하코네 날씨 및 옷차림 팁</b></span></p><!-- } SE-TEXT --></div>

                <div class="se-component se-text se-l-default" id="SE-66827634-c300-47cd-9c10-cad7e8ad97e6">
                    <div class="se-component-content">
                        <div class="se-section se-section-text se-l-default">
                            <div class="se-module se-module-text">
                                    <!-- SE-TEXT { --><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-04a15c90-491d-4202-ada1-05a7e8c56a5f"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-ea678ffe-fdfe-4b7a-b407-63fdc1a319a3">하코네유모토 지역은 평균적으로 봄: 15℃, 여름: 25℃, 가을: 15℃, 겨울: 7℃입니다.</span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-b36b35d1-9e0d-483e-b98c-19e10664b7c7"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-127065e5-c374-4afa-9030-048412285f20">단 아시노코 호수, 오와쿠다니 지역 등 해발이 높은 곳은 3~4℃ 기온이 낮고 날씨 변화가 잦습니다. </span></p><ul class="se-text-list se-text-list-type-bullet-disc"><li class="se-text-list-item"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-9c558422-59eb-4cc3-9ca1-0774638d29b9"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-3a3e256e-3902-4f14-9ed1-1677fe74b036"><b>봄: </b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-0a92e5ab-903d-430a-91ac-491e74cd3a1a">3월의 평균 기온은 도쿄와 같은 정도이지만 때때로 두꺼운 코트가 필요합니다.</span></p></li></ul><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-f61dd48e-b92f-4128-9023-634c8fa7c3bf"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-5ce7bef7-6c10-4315-91d4-6b95a9d08d9c">4, 5월은 따뜻해지지만 자켓이 있으면 안심입니다.</span></p><ul class="se-text-list se-text-list-type-bullet-disc"><li class="se-text-list-item"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-80639a15-06d4-4165-bdc5-6aa49891e67b"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-ff14d872-7c2b-4fc8-8beb-27a60ac1f965"><b>여름:</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-4d0a1ac6-0142-4158-bc56-45940d120d07"> 대부분 반팔로 지낼 수 있지만 얇은 외투가 있으면 안심입니다.</span></p></li><li class="se-text-list-item"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-2a6b066f-49bf-4fe1-853e-266244099544"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-2500d5a1-9002-40d8-b095-1c5056c18a25"><b>가을:</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-b0b446b5-d366-45f3-a0e9-8d9411938580"> 긴팔 셔츠와 외투. 어떤 날은 두꺼운 코트가 필요합니다. 10월 말 ~ 11월 중순이 단풍시즌으로 가장 아름답습니다.</span></p></li><li class="se-text-list-item"><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-239dd0c1-27fd-4048-8673-387016b5cea5"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff-   " id="SE-a6567f07-e4dd-423a-9b11-c745ac1ba1f0"><b>겨울:</b></span><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-ba3bcb0f-5f2b-44ba-833a-db1ec9b98fe2"> 두꺼운 코트가 필요합니다. 해발 차이가 있기 때문에 여러 벌을 겹쳐 있는 등</span></p></li></ul><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-d5762ae1-7dda-4e2f-b9c1-9e7c2f01562c"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-120415eb-b8f7-4a50-a0a4-aa536d680bf2">방한 대책을 제대로 합시다.</span></p><p class="se-text-paragraph se-text-paragraph-align- " style="" id="SE-701a6942-96ff-4629-a606-a46550eeaf60"><span style="color:#000000;" class="se-fs-fs19 se-ff- se-weight-unset  " id="SE-13f35a19-fa6a-4f51-bff0-66811bd952bc">​</span></p><!-- } SE-TEXT -->
                            </div>
